created: 2026-04-20
owner: yubo
---

# 路线图 · v1.0 执行计划（Roadmap）

## 本文件定位

**路线图 = 前瞻性的分阶段交付计划**——回答"接下来按什么顺序做、做到什么程度算一个阶段达成"。

与项目中其他两个相关文档的语义分工：

| 文档 | 语义 | 粒度 | 方向 | 变更频率 | 用法 |
|------|------|------|------|---------|------|
| `.42cog/meta/meta.md §项目里程碑` | **版本里程碑**（release milestone） | 大（MVP / v1.0 / v2.0） | 前瞻但粗 | 季度级 | 回答"项目要做到哪里" |
| `.42cog/work/roadmap-v1.0.md`（本文件） | **执行路线图**（roadmap） | 中（m1 / m2 / m3 + 判据） | 前瞻且可执行 | 周级 | 回答"下一个交付是什么、何时算达成" |
| `.42cog/work/milestones.md` | **事件日志**（activity log / changelog） | 小（单条交付） | 事后 | 每次实质进展 | 回答"到今天为止已经做过什么" |

**三个文档的关系**：meta 锁方向 → roadmap 拆阶段 → milestones 记流水。任何一层缺失，项目就会陷入"没路标（meta 缺）/ 没路线（roadmap 缺）/ 没账本（milestones 缺）"。

**为什么需要显式分工**：此前 meta.md §项目里程碑 与 milestones.md 都用了"里程碑"一词，但语义错位——meta 的"里程碑"是版本节点（3 条），milestones.md 的"里程碑"是事件日志（N 条）。两者一词双义导致"我做的事算不算里程碑"这种反复无解的问题。本路线图出现后，两份文档各回其位：meta 管愿景、milestones 管账本、roadmap 管执行。

---

## 当前位置（20...(truncated)
```

## 🤖 Assistant [16:10:43 +08:00]

现在我有完整的上下文了，直接给你结论。

---

**还不是 `design-ui-design` 的时机。**

当前实际位置：

| 状态 | 内容 |
|------|------|
| ✓ m1 判据 1-5 | 全部完成（规约/DB/Auth/AI/Inngest 骨架） |
| ✓ m1 判据 7 | milestones.md 补登 + roadmap-v1.0.md 落盘（d85c400） |
| **❌ m1 判据 6** | PG 6 触发器契约测代码已写好，但 **Docker Desktop 未运行**，`test:contract` 21 个测试全跳过 |

m1 还差最后一步没闭合，原因是 Docker Desktop 没跑。

---

**正确顺序：**

1. **现在该做的**：启动 Docker Desktop → `bun run test:contract` 跑通 → m1 达成（6/7→7/7）
2. **然后是** m2-MAS-1：后端（POST /api/manuscripts → POST /api/tasks → Inngest 真实 LLM 调用 → 三维度写入 DB）
3. **MAS-1 后端完成后才进** `design-ui-design`——此时才有明确的数据结构和 API 契约供 UI 设计参考

`design-ui-design` 在 MAS-1 后端骨架没有之前进去，会设计一个没有数据接口支撑的空壳页面——而 spec 里的三维度展示（confidence/match_status/result 维度）需要先有 `/api/tasks/[id]` 的响应结构才能合理设计组件。

---

**最近要做：** 你打开 Docker Desktop，我立刻跑 `bun run test:contract` 闭合 m1。

  → 任务完成，N 天后自动销毁（CS-04）
  → 日后回看报告，版本戳依然完整（CS-03）
```

#### MS-L-03：上传书稿文件（多格式）

**CS**：CS-01 | **Type**：Light | **Priority**：P0 | **Story Points**：3 | **MVP 复用度**：已有

**User Story**:
作为一个 **带着书稿来校对的编辑**，

- **AC3**：非白名单格式直接拦截并提示，不进入解析管线
- **AC4**：上传过程中可取消，未完成上传的文件立即从服务器删除（对齐 real.md #3）
- **AC5**：超过单文件上限（默认 20MB）给出明确错误，**不得**静默截断

**User-Perceivable Changes**:
- **Before**：空的上传区，手上有散稿
- **During**：拖入，进度条滚动
- **After**：看到卡片"书稿《XX》已解析 / 287 段 / 找到疑似引文 63 条"

**Constraints**:
- notes #3 —— PDF 竖排需检测方向；CJK Ext B-G 字符不丢

#### MS-L-05：预估费用 + 二次确认 + 发起任务

**CS**：CS-01 | **Type**：Light | **Priority**：P0 | **Story Points**：3 | **MVP 复用度**：全新

**User Story**:
作为一个 **按量付费的编辑**，
我想 **在发起任务前先看到清晰的费用预估**，
以便 **对成本有可控预期，不怕账单刺客**。

**Light Story 评估**:
- **起始状态**：上传了书稿和参考，但不知要花多少钱
- **转折点**：系统给出预估 `¥X.XX ± Y%`，附拆分（模型单价 × 引文数估算 × 调用次数）
- **终止状态**：确认后任务启动
- **情感弧**：不确定 → 透明 → 放心确认

**Acceptance Criteria**:
- **AC1**：点击"发起校对"后弹预估卡片，包含：预估费用 / 预估时长 / 引文条数估算 / 拆分公式
- **AC2**：预估 < ¥50 直接确认即可；≥ ¥50 强制二次确认（real.md #6）
- **AC3**：预估卡片底部显示"实际费用将在运行中 SSE 推送；超预估 1.5× 自动暂停"（引到 MS-D-04）
- **AC4**：确认后生成 `校对任务` 记录落库（cog.md 实体），含 `task_id` + 版本戳三元组占位（MAS-5 填充）
- **AC5**：取消后**不**产生费用，未调用 API

**Perceivable Changes**:
- **Before**：不知成本
- **During**：看到拆分明细
- **After**：已启动，进入 SSE 观察态

**Constraints**:
- real.md #6 —— 成本上限与二次确认
- notes #4 —— 任务状态必须持久化（不能只在内存）

**Dependencies**:
- Requires：MS-L-04
- Enables：MS-L-06

---

#### MS-L-06：SSE 实时观察进度（三段式里程碑）

**CS**：CS-01 | **Type**：Light | **Priority**：P0 | **S...(truncated)
```

📤 Result:

```
你是一位专业的中文学术书稿引用提取专家。你的任务是从书稿文本中识别并提取所有引用内容。

## 书稿格式说明

书稿文本以分段格式传入，每段以 `[段落N]` 标记开头（N为段落编号）。提取引用时请记录该引用出现在哪个段落编号中。

## 引用类型识别

请识别以下形式的引用：
1. **引号引用**：使用中文引号（"…"或"…"）或书名号内嵌引号括起来的文字
2. **明确标注的引用**：包含以下引导语的内容：
   - "引自"、"摘自"、"出自"、"见"
   - "据X所言"、"X指出"、"X认为"、"X说"、"X写道"、"X提到"、"X强调"
   - "正如X所说"、"如X所言"、"按X的说法"
   - "X在《书名》中指出/写道/认为"
3. **间接引用**：作者转述他人观点，即使未用引号，但有明确出处标注

## 提取要求

- 提取引用的原始文字（保持原样，不做修改）
- 提取引用前后各约100字的上下文（用于理解引用语境），上下文中不包含 [段落N] 标记
- 识别作者对该引用的解释或评论（通常紧随引用之后或之前）
- 识别该引用来自哪部原始文献（如《论语》《周易》《史记》等），填入 source_work 字段
- 从 [段落N] 标记中读取该引用所在的段落编号，填入 para_index 字段
- 识别该引用所属的章节（从段落标题或上下文推断），填入 chapter 字段
- 若文中有页码、章节、脚注编号等位置信息，一并提取至 location_hint

## 输出格式

严格按照以下JSON格式输出，不要输出任何其他文字：

```json
[
  {
    "quote": "被引用的原始文字（完整保留引号内或明确标注的内容）",
    "context_before": "引用前约100字的文本（不含[段落N]标记）",
    "context_after": "引用后约100字的文本（不含[段落N]标记）",
    "author_explanation": "作者对该引用的解释、评价或分析（若无明显解释则填空字符串）",
    "location_hint": "页码、脚注编号、章节信息等位置提示（若无则填空字符串）",
    "source_work": "被引用文献名称，如《论语》《周易》（无法判断则填空字符串...(truncated)
```

## 🤖 Assistant [16:44:51 +08:00]

}

📤 Result:

```
/**
 * 客观置信度三信号融合
 *
 * spec-system-architecture ADR-007 · real.md #2（置信度不得由 AI 自评）
 *
 * 设计要点：
 *   - LLM 返回的任何 "confidence" / "score" / "certainty" 字段必须被**丢弃**
 *   - confidence = w1·refHit + w2·locationValid + w3·crossModel
 *   - v1.0 配置：w1=0.5 · w2=0.5 · w3=0（跨模型费用翻倍，v1.1 再开启）
 *   - 算法版本化进 report_snapshot.versionStamp.confidenceAlgoVersion
 *
 * 不做的：
 *   - 不接受 LLM 的置信度声明（哪怕是 0/100 确数）
 *   - 不做"模糊折扣"或"多样性惩罚"（无来源的主观加减）
 */

export const CONFIDENCE_ALGO_VERSION = 'v1.0' as const;
export type ConfidenceAlgoVersion = typeof CONFIDENCE_ALGO_VERSION;

export const CONFIDENCE_WEIGHTS = {
  refHit: 0.5,
  locationValid: 0.5,
  crossModel: 0,
} as const;

export interface ConfidenceSignals {
  /** 引文与参考文献的归一化相似度 ∈ [0,1]；未命中=0；等值完全命中=1 */
  refHit: number;
  /** 返回定位（书名/章节/段落）是否真实存在于参考元数据 ∈ {0,1} */
  locationValid: 0 | 1;
  /** 跨模型一致性 ∈ [0,1]；v1.0 一律填 0（权重=0，不参与） */
  crossModel: number;
}

export interface ConfidenceResult {
  value: number;
  signals: ConfidenceSignals;
  weights: type...(truncated)
```

/**
 * Inngest 客户端单例
 *

      "location": "章节 / 段落 / 页码（若可推断）"
    }
  ],
  "overall_remark": "给编辑的整体比对说明（非判决）；全部一致则填写\"本条引文在所比对维度上与原文一致\""
}
```

## 字段说明

- `match_status` 取值枚举：`"match"`（一致）/ `"partial"`（部分一致）/ `"mismatch"`（不一致）/ `"not_found"`（原文中未找到对应内容）
- `differences`：仅客观描述观察到的差异，不使用判决性词汇（如"有瑕"/"失当"）
- `original_text`：仅在字词准确性维度使用，填写原文对应段落
- `editor_suggestion`：给编辑参考的可能修改方向，**不是系统的判决**；无需修改时填空字符串
- `reference_hits`：记录原文中能匹配到的片段（支持多处命中；异文、转引场景可有多条）；完全未找到则为空数组
- `overall_remark`：保持事实描述；严禁使用判决性措辞
- **不输出 confidence / score 等自评字段**：置信度由系统基于参考命中度与定位有效性客观计算

## 示例

**输入示例：**
- 引用文字："学而时习之，不亦乐乎"
- 作者解释：孔子认为学习应当快乐，强调学习的愉悦感
- 原文内容：子曰："学而时习之，不亦说乎？有朋自远方来，不亦乐乎？"

**输出示例：**
```json
{
  "quote": "学而时习之，不亦乐乎",
  "text_accuracy": {
    "match_status": "mismatch",
    "differences": "原文作\"不亦说乎\"，书稿引文末字作\"乐乎\"；\"乐乎\"在原文中属下句\"有朋自远方来\"之结语",
    "original_text": "学而时习之，不亦说乎",
    "variant_note": ""
  },
  "interpretation_accuracy": {
    "match_status": "partial",
    "differences": "作者将\"说（悦）\"释为学习之愉悦，方向一致；但将\"乐乎\"与学习之情境合并，与原...(truncated)
```

📤 Result:

```
import { readFileSync } from 'node:fs';
import { createHash } from 'node:crypto';
import path from 'node:path';

// spec-coding §10.1 · real.md #7 · ADR-012
// prompts/v1/ 是版本冻结资产，启动时 SHA256 校验
// PROMPT_VERSION 在此升级时同步建 prompts/v2/，不得原地改 v1/

export type PromptKey = 'extract' | 'verify' | 'map';

export const PROMPT_VERSION = 'v1' as const;

export interface PromptRecord {
  readonly text: string;
  readonly sha256: string;
  readonly version: typeof PROMPT_VERSION;
  readonly key: PromptKey;
}

const cache = new Map<PromptKey, PromptRecord>();

export function loadPromptRaw(key: PromptKey): PromptRecord {
  const cached = cache.get(key);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const filePath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'prompts', PROMPT_VERSION, `${key}.txt`);
  const text = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
  const sha256 = createHash('sha256').update(text).digest('hex');
  const record: PromptRecord = { text, sha256, version: PROMPT_VERSION, key };
  cache.set(key, record);
  return record;
...(truncated)
```

📤 Result:

```
export function stripLlmSelfScores<T extends Record<string, unknown>>(raw: T): T {
  const BLOCKED = new Set(['confidence', 'score', 'certainty', 'probability']);
  const out = {} as Record<string, unknown>;
  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(raw)) {
    if (BLOCKED.has(k.toLowerCase())) continue;
    out[k] = v;
  }
  return out as T;
}

function clamp01(n: number): number {
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return 0;
  if (n < 0) return 0;
  if (n > 1) return 1;
  return n;
}
```

1	import { del, put } from '@vercel/blob';

3	export async function uploadManuscriptBlob(
4	  filename: string,
5	  buffer: Buffer,
6	  mimeType: string,

8	  const blob = await put(`manuscripts/${Date.now()}-${filename}`, buffer, {
9	    access: 'private',
10	    contentType: mimeType,
11	  });

## 🤖 Assistant [17:43:49 +08:00]

`BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` 只有 placeholder，没有真实 token。Vercel Blob 上传会失败。两条路：

**A.** 先用 Vercel CLI 拉真实 token（`vercel env pull`）
**B.** 暂时跳过 Blob，把书稿直接存 DB（text 字段），不上云存储

Vercel CLI 没有安装（开头提示过）。先改个策略——上传阶段绕过 Blob，直接把文件内容存在 manuscript 表（blobUrl/blobPathname 填 local-only 占位），这样其他流程（解析 → Inngest → 报告）都能跑通。

   - Session's core goal: build `quote-check` v1.0, completing m1 then starting m2-MAS-1

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Project**: `quote-check` — Chinese academic manuscript proofreading tool, three-dimensional (字词/解释/语境) quote verification against reference texts
   - **Stack**: Next.js 15.1.6, React 19, Drizzle ORM + Neon PostgreSQL, Inngest 3.27, Better Auth 0.7.5, AI SDK + DeepSeek via SiliconFlow, Tailwind v4, Vercel Blob
   - **Roadmap**: m1 (基建) → m2 (MAS-1~4 校对主流程) → m3 (上线闭环)
   - **Three-doc system**: meta.md (version vision) / roadmap-v1.0.md (execution plan) / milestones.md (activity log)
   - **MAS-1 判据**: POST /api/manuscripts → POST /api/tasks → Inngest proofread-run real LLM → verification_result DB write → /api/reports/:id JSON → UI三维度卡片
   - **Idempotency**: `buildResultIdempotencyKey({taskId, quoteId, attemptN})` for DB unique constraint
   - **Confidence**: Three-signal objective scoring (refHit + locationValid + crossModel, weights w1=0.5/w2=0.5/w3=0)
   - **Inngest steps**: load-task → moderation-gate → extract-quotes → save-quotes → verify-each-quote (serial, DG-m2.1) → freeze-report
   - **testcontainers-pg**: Used for PG trigger contract tests (Docker required)
   - **exactOptionalPropertyTypes**: TypeScript strict mode affecting optional field handling

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`lib/parsers/manuscript.ts`** (new) — Parse txt/md/docx to paragraph arrays using mammoth for docx
     ```typescript
     export async function parseManuscript(buffer: Buffer, mimeType: string, filename: string): Promise<ParseResult>
     // Supports text/plain, text/markdown, .docx via mammoth
     // Returns { paragraphs: ParsedParagraph[], charCount: number, mimeType: string }
     ```

   - **`lib/storage/blob.ts`** (new) — Vercel Blob upload/delete wrapper
     ```typescript
     export async function uploadManuscriptBlob(filename, buffer, mimeType): Promise<{ url, pathname }>
     // access: 'public' (v0.27.0 doesn't support 'private')
     ```

   - **`lib/services/manuscript.ts`** (new) — DB operations
     ```typescript
     export async function createManuscript(values): Promise<Manuscript>
     export async function saveParagraphs(manuscriptId, paragraphs): Promise<void>
     export async function markManuscriptParsed(id, charCount): Promise<void>
     export async function getManuscript(id): Promise<Manuscript | undefined>
     ```

   - **`lib/services/task.ts`** (new) — Core DB operations
     ```typescript
     export async function createTask({userId, manuscriptId, referenceIds?}): Promise<Task>
     // ttlExpiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) (required field)
     export async function getTask(id): Promise<Task | undefined>
     export async function updateTaskStatus(id, status): Promise<void>
     export async function updateTaskProgress(id, updates): Promise<void>
     export async function getTaskContext(taskId): Promise<{task, paragraphs} | null>
     export async function saveQuotes(manuscriptId, rows): Promise<Quote[]>
     // Uses spread conditional: ...(r.sourceWorkHint !== undefined ? { sourceWorkHint: r.sourceWorkHint } : {})
     export async function saveVerificationResult(row): Promise<VerificationResult | null>
     // Uses .onConflictDoNothing() for idempotency
     export async function createReportSnapshot(values): Promise<void>
     export async function getReport(taskId): Promise<ReportRow | null>
     ```

   - **`app/api/manuscripts/route.ts`** (new) — POST upload
     ```typescript
     // Local Blob bypass when token contains 'placeholder':
     const blobToken = process.env['BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN'] ?? '';
     if (!blobToken.includes('placeholder')) {
       const uploaded = await uploadManuscriptBlob(file.name, buffer, mimeType);

     }
     ```

   - **`app/api/tasks/route.ts`** (new) — POST create task + Inngest send
     - Creates task, updates to VERIFYING, sends `task/proofread.requested` event

   - **`inngest/functions/proofread-run.ts`** (major rewrite) — Real LLM implementation
     ```typescript
     // Zod schemas for LLM output
     const ExtractOutputSchema = z.array(ExtractedQuoteSchema)
     const VerifyOutputSchema = z.object({...})
     
     // Steps: load-task, moderation-gate (stub), extract-quotes (real LLM),
     //        save-quotes, verify-each-quote (serial loop), freeze-report
     
     // Multi-strategy JSON extraction:
     const jsonCandidates: string[] = [];
     const codeBlockMatch = rawOutput.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/);
     if (codeBlockMatch?.[1]) jsonCandidates.push(codeBlockMatch[1].trim());
     const braceMatch = rawOutput.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
     if (braceMatch?.[0]) jsonCandidates.push(braceMatch[0]);
     jsonCandidates.push(rawOutput.trim());
     ```
     
     **Currently being edited** — adding Chinese value normalization:
     ```typescript
     function normMatchStatus(raw: unknown, type: 'text' | 'dim'): string {
       const s = String(raw ?? '').toLowerCase().trim();
       if (s.includes('not_applicable') || s.includes('无需') || s.includes('不适用')) return 'not_applicable';
       // ...maps Chinese to English
     }
     const MatchStatusCoerce = z.unknown().transform((v) => normMatchStatus(v, 'text'));
     const DimStatusCoerce = z.unknown().transform((v) => normMatchStatus(v, 'dim'));
     ```

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **`access: 'private'` in Vercel Blob**: @vercel/blob 0.27.0 only supports `'public'` → Changed to `'public'`
   - **`ttlExpiresAt` missing in task insert**: Required field in schema → Added `ttlExpiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)`
   - **`exactOptionalPropertyTypes` with `undefined` vs null**: Used spread conditional `...(r.sourceWorkHint !== undefined ? { sourceWorkHint: r.sourceWorkHint } : {})` instead of passing `undefined`
   - **`Array<T>` lint rule**: Changed to `T[]` syntax throughout services/task.ts (required Python sed due to my earlier replace_all mistake corrupting the file with `/* Array< replaced */`)
   - **`NextRequest` type-only imports**: Changed to `import type { NextRequest }` in all API routes
   - **`and()` import unused in services/task.ts**: Removed import, changed `and(eq(...))` to just `eq(...)`
   - **`suggestedCorrection: undefined`**: Needed to omit the key entirely (exactOptionalPropertyTypes) → removed the field
   - **Confidence breakdown weights key names**: Schema expects `{ w1, w2, w3 }` not `{ refHit, locationValid, crossModel }` → Fixed mapping
   - **`stripLlmSelfScores` wrong usage**: Function takes `Record<string, unknown>` not `string` → Removed from the string rawOutput context
   - **`isModerationRejection` unused import**: Removed
   - **Inngest dev server needs proxy bypass**: `env -u http_proxy -u https_proxy curl` for all localhost calls
   - **LLM returns Chinese `"无需比对"` instead of `"not_applicable"`**: Root cause of 4/8 failures in E2E test → Currently fixing with `normMatchStatus()` function and Zod `.transform()`

8. Current Work:
   Immediately before the summary request, I was fixing a critical bug in `inngest/functions/proofread-run.ts`:

   **Root cause**: LLM returns `"match_status": "无需比对"` (Chinese for "not applicable") in `interpretation_accuracy` and `context_appropriateness` fields, because `prompts/v1/verify.txt` uses Chinese to describe the "无需比对" case. Our Zod schema only accepted English enum values, so `VerifyOutputSchema.safeParse()` was failing, causing 4/8 quotes to be stored as "LLM 返回格式异常".

   **Fix being applied** to `inngest/functions/proofread-run.ts`:
   ```typescript
   function normMatchStatus(raw: unknown, type: 'text' | 'dim'): 'match' | 'partial' | 'mismatch' | 'not_found' | 'not_applicable' {
     const s = String(raw ?? '').toLowerCase().trim();
     if (s.includes('not_found') || s.includes('未找到') || ...) return 'not_found';
     if (s.includes('not_applicable') || s.includes('无需') || ...) return 'not_applicable';
     // ...
   }
   const MatchStatusCoerce = z.unknown().transform((v) => normMatchStatus(v, 'text'));
   const DimStatusCoerce = z.unknown().transform((v) => normMatchStatus(v, 'dim'));
   ```
   
   Also updated `llmMatchToDb()` and `llmMatchToVerdict()` to accept `string` instead of narrow union types, and added explicit return types to ternary expressions for verdictInterpretation and verdictContext.

   The edits were complete but **typecheck and lint had NOT been run yet** when the summary was requested.

📤 Result:

```
1	import type { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
2	import { NextResponse } from 'next/server';
3	
4	import { inngest } from '@/inngest/client';
5	import { auth } from '@/lib/auth';
6	import { getManuscript } from '@/lib/services/manuscript';
7	import { createTask, updateTaskStatus } from '@/lib/services/task';
8	
9	export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
10	  const session = await auth.api.getSession({ headers: req.headers });
11	  if (!session?.user?.id) {
12	    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
13	  }
14

Now I have a clear picture. Critical gaps:
- **No `reference_paragraph` table** — references only store Blob URLs + contentHash; passage-level storage + trigram index is paragraph-only.

- **map.txt prompt exists** but isn't wired; requires source_works list as input.

1	import { del, put } from '@vercel/blob';
2	
3	export async function uploadManuscriptBlob(
4	  filename: string,
5	  buffer: Buffer,
6	  mimeType: string,
7	): Promise<{ url: string; pathname: string }> {
8	  const blob = await put(`manuscripts/${Date.now()}-${filename}`, buffer, {
9	    access: 'public',
10	    contentType: mimeType,
11	  });
12	  return { url: blob.url, pathname: blob.pathname };
13	}
14	
15	export async function deleteBlobByUrl(url: string): Promise<void> {
16	  await del(url);
17	}
18	
```

📤 Result:

```
140	EXECUTE FUNCTION prevent_prompt_version_mutation();
141	
142	-- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
143	-- I-01: task.reference_ids GIN 索引
144	--   drizzle-kit 对数组 GIN 无原生语法
145	-- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
146	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_task_reference_ids_gin
147	  ON task USING GIN (reference_ids);
148	
149	-- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
150	-- I-02: pg_trgm 扩展 + paragraph / quote trigram 索引
151	--   近似检索辅助（n-gram 匹配），中文分词不走 tsvector
152	-- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
153	CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm;

1	/**
2	 * 客观置信度三信号融合
3	 *
4	 * spec-system-architecture ADR-007 · real.md #2（置信度不得由 AI 自评）
5	 *
6	 * 设计要点：
7	 *   - LLM 返回的任何 "confidence" / "score" / "certainty" 字段必须被**丢弃**
8	 *   - confidence = w1·refHit + w2·locationValid + w3·crossModel
9	 *   - v1.0 配置：w1=0.5 · w2=0.5 · w3=0（跨模型费用翻倍，v1.1 再开启）
10	 *   - 算法版本化进 report_snapshot.versionStamp.confidenceAlgoVersion
11	 *
12	 * 不做的：
13	 *   - 不接受 LLM 的置信度声明（哪怕是 0/100 确数）
14	 *   - 不做"模糊折扣"或"多样性惩罚"（无来源的主观加减）
15	 */
16	
17	export const CONFIDENCE_ALGO_VERSION = 'v1.0' as const;
18	export type ConfidenceAlgoVersion = typeof CONFIDENCE_ALGO_VERSION;
19	
20	export const CONFIDENCE_WEIGHTS = {
21	  refHit: 0.5,
22	  locationValid: 0.5,
23	  crossModel: 0,
24	} as const;
25	
26	export interface ConfidenceSignals {
27	  /** 引文与参考文献的归一化相似度 ∈ [0,1]；未命中=0；等值完全命中=1 */
28	  refHit: number;
29	  /** 返回定位（书名/章节/段落）是否真实存在于参考元数据 ∈ {0,1} */
30	  locationValid: 0 | 1;
31	  /** 跨模型一致性 ∈ [0,1]；v1.0 一律填 0（权重=0，不参与） */
32	  crossModel: number;
33	}

4	import { auth } from '@/lib/auth';
5	import { getReport } from '@/lib/services/task';
6	
7	export async function GET(req: NextRequest, { params }: { params: Promise<{ taskId: string }> }) {
8	  const session = await auth.api.getSession({ headers: req.headers });
9	  if (!session?.user?.id) {
10	    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
11	  }
12	
13	  const { taskId } = await params;
14	  const report = await getReport(taskId);
15	  if (!report) return NextResponse.json({ error: '报告不存在' }, { status: 404 });
16	  if (report.task.userId !== session.user.id) {
17	    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Forbidden' }, { status: 403 });
18	  }
19	
20	  return NextResponse.json({
21	    taskId: report.task.id,
22	    displayId: report.task.displayId,
23	    status: report.task.status,
24	    totalQuotes: report.task.totalQuotes,

import { serve } from 'inngest/next';

import { inngest } from '@/inngest/client';
import { pingFn } from '@/inngest/functions/ping';
import { proofreadRunFn } from '@/inngest/functions/proofread-run';
import { env } from '@/lib/env';

/**
 * Inngest serve handler（GET/POST/PUT）
 *
 * - 路径：/api/inngest（Inngest Cloud 注册时的默认 URL）
 * - GET：返回函数清单 + 版本，供 Inngest dev server & Cloud dashboard 自省
 * - POST：接收 Inngest Cloud 投递的事件，调用对应函数
 * - PUT：sync 端点，Inngest Cloud 推送"重新注册函数清单"请求
 * - signingKey：生产环境强校验 HMAC 签名（env.INNGEST_SIGNING_KEY）；
 *   本地 dev 可留空，inngest-cli 会跳过签名
 */
export const { GET, POST, PUT } = serve({
  client: inngest,
  functions: [pingFn, proofreadRunFn],
  signingKey: env.INNGEST_SIGNING_KEY,
});
```

## 👤 User [22:22:10 +08:00]

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The session had two phases:
   - **MAS-1 completion**: Confirm the `normMatchStatus` Chinese normalization fix works, run E2E test, commit, and update roadmap/milestones
   - **MAS-2 implementation** (参考为准绳): Plan and implement reference document upload + pg_trgm paragraph-level retrieval + four-state match (MATCH/PARTIAL_MATCH/NOT_MATCH/NOT_FOUND_IN_REF) + result_reference_hit M:N writes + UI extension

   User decisions for MAS-2 (via AskUserQuestion):
   - Retrieval: **pg_trgm 段落级** (add `reference_paragraph` table with GIN trigram)
   - map.txt: **不接入，延后** (defer to MAS-2b; only needs lint check)
   - UI scope: **扩展 /upload 页** (extend existing upload page, not a separate library)

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **pg_trgm similarity()**: `similarity(text_normalized, $query) > threshold` for passage retrieval from reference paragraphs
   - **reference_paragraph table**: New table mirroring `paragraph`, stores `textNormalized` (CJK normalized via `normalizeForCompare`) for trigram indexing
   - **GIN trigram index I-03**: `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ref_para_text_trgm ON reference_paragraph USING GIN (text_normalized gin_trgm_ops)`
   - **Four-state matchStatus decision logic**: if no refs uploaded → undefined (LLM decides); no paragraphs matched → NOT_FOUND_IN_REF; topSim ≥ 0.75 → MATCH; topSim ≥ 0.4 → PARTIAL_MATCH; else → NOT_MATCH
   - **DG-m2.2 thresholds**: SIMILARITY_MATCH_THRESHOLD=0.75, SIMILARITY_PARTIAL_THRESHOLD=0.4 (empirical, need real corpus validation)
   - **Neon HTTP array parameter issue**: `db.execute(sql`...ANY(${uuidArray})`)` causes "malformed array literal"; fix is to use raw `neon` tagged template literal directly which serializes JS arrays correctly
   - **normMatchStatus**: Chinese→English enum normalization in proofread-run.ts (MAS-1 fix confirmed working)
   - **result_reference_hit M:N**: One row per (result, reference) pair, `hit=true/false` proving reference was scanned
   - **copyright declaration**: Required checkbox before reference upload (real.md #5)
   - **load-references step (S1.5)**: New Inngest step between load-task and moderation-gate

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **`lib/db/schema.ts`** — Added `referenceParagraph` table after `reference` table; updated `referenceRelations` to include `paragraphs: many(referenceParagraph)`; added `referenceParagraphRelations`:
     ```typescript
     export const referenceParagraph = pgTable('reference_paragraph', {
       id: uuid('id').primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
       referenceId: uuid('reference_id').notNull().references(() => reference.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
       seq: integer('seq').notNull(),
       displayId: varchar('display_id', { length: 64 }).notNull(),
       text: text('text').notNull(),
       textNormalized: text('text_normalized').notNull(),
       textHash: varchar('text_hash', { length: 64 }).notNull(),
       createdAt: timestamp('created_at', { withTimezone: true }).defaultNow().notNull(),
     }, (t) => ({
       referenceSeqIdx: index('idx_ref_para_reference_seq').on(t.referenceId, t.seq),
     }));
     ```

   - **`lib/db/types.ts`** — Added `referenceParagraph` import and `ReferenceParagraph`/`NewReferenceParagraph` exports

   - **`lib/db/migrations/0002_simple_luckman.sql`** — Auto-generated by `bun run db:generate`; creates `reference_paragraph` table in Neon

     ```

       // WHERE deletedAt IS NULL
     ```

   - **`lib/storage/blob.ts`** — Refactored to shared `uploadToBlob` helper; added `uploadReferenceBlob` with `references/` prefix:
     ```typescript
     async function uploadToBlob(path, buffer, mimeType) { const blob = await put(path, buffer, {access: 'public', contentType: mimeType}); return {url: blob.url, pathname: blob.pathname}; }
     export async function uploadManuscriptBlob(filename, buffer, mimeType) { return uploadToBlob(`manuscripts/${Date.now()}-${filename}`, buffer, mimeType); }
     export async function uploadReferenceBlob(filename, buffer, mimeType) { return uploadToBlob(`references/${Date.now()}-${filename}`, buffer, mimeType); }
     ```

   - **`lib/ai/confidence.ts`** — Added DG-m2.2 thresholds:
     ```typescript
     export const SIMILARITY_MATCH_THRESHOLD = 0.75;
     export const SIMILARITY_PARTIAL_THRESHOLD = 0.4;
     ```

   - **`lib/ai/retrieval.ts`** (NEW) — pg_trgm retrieval using raw neon client (CURRENT STATE after fix):
     ```typescript
     import { neon } from '@neondatabase/serverless';
     import { env } from '@/lib/env';
     import { normalizeForCompare } from '@/lib/text/normalize';
     
     const rawSql = neon(env.DATABASE_URL);
     
     export interface PassageHit {
       referenceId: string; paragraphId: string; paragraphSeq: number; text: string; similarity: number;
     }
     
     export async function retrievePassagesForQuote({ quoteText, referenceIds, topK=3, minSimilarity=0.3 }): Promise<PassageHit[]> {
       if (referenceIds.length === 0 || !quoteText.trim()) return [];
       const normalized = normalizeForCompare(quoteText, 'simplified');
       const rows = await rawSql`
         SELECT id, reference_id, seq, text, similarity(text_normalized, ${normalized}) AS sim
         FROM reference_paragraph
         WHERE reference_id = ANY(${referenceIds})
           AND similarity(text_normalized, ${normalized}) > ${minSimilarity}
         ORDER BY sim DESC
         LIMIT ${topK}
       ` as { id: string; reference_id: string; seq: number; text: string; sim: string }[];
       return rows.map(r => ({ referenceId: r.reference_id, paragraphId: r.id, paragraphSeq: r.seq, text: r.text, similarity: Number(r.sim) }));
     }
     ```

   - **`app/api/references/route.ts`** (NEW) — POST upload + GET list:
     - POST: auth → formData(file + canonicalName + role + copyrightDeclared) → validate copyrightDeclared → parseManuscript → uploadReferenceBlob (placeholder bypass) → createReference → saveReferenceParagraphs → markReferenceParsed → {referenceId, displayId, canonicalName, paragraphCount, charCount}
     - GET: auth → listUserReferences → {references: [...]}

   - **`lib/services/task.ts`** — Added `reference` and `resultReferenceHit` imports; added `saveReferenceHits` function using spread conditional for optional fields; extended `ReportRow` to include `referenceHits: ReferenceHitRow[]`; extended `getReport()` to LEFT JOIN resultReferenceHit + reference (hit=true only), group into Map by resultId:
     ```typescript
     export async function saveReferenceHits(resultId: string, hits: {referenceId, hit, snippet?, similarity?, retrievalMethod?}[]): Promise<void> {
       await db.insert(resultReferenceHit).values(hits.map(h => ({
         resultId, referenceId: h.referenceId, hit: h.hit,
         ...(h.snippet !== undefined ? { snippet: h.snippet } : {}),
         ...(h.similarity !== undefined ? { similarity: String(h.similarity) } : {}),
         ...(h.retrievalMethod !== undefined ? { retrievalMethod: h.retrievalMethod } : {}),
       }))).onConflictDoNothing();
     }
     ```

   import { env } from '@/lib/env';
   const rawSql = neon(env.DATABASE_URL);
   const rows = await rawSql`
     SELECT ... WHERE reference_id = ANY(${referenceIds}) ...
   ` as { id: string; reference_id: string; seq: number; text: string; sim: string }[];
   ```

import * as OpenCC from 'opencc-js';
import { VARIANT_MAP, LIGATURE_PRESERVE } from './variants';

// spec-coding §9 · notes #3 · ADR-014
// 所有引文 / 参考 / 用户输入的比对必经此函数
// 不允许在业务代码里直接 str.replace 做繁简转换

export type NormalizeMode = 'simplified' | 'traditional' | 'preserve';

const t2s = OpenCC.Converter({ from: 't', to: 'cn' });
const s2t = OpenCC.Converter({ from: 'cn', to: 't' });

// OpenCC 't'→'cn' 会把乾/隆/元 的"乾"误简为"干"——对文史文本不合适
// 这里对几个经典语境做回补（宁可漏简，不可乱简）
const POST_SIMPLIFY_FIXUPS: readonly (readonly [RegExp, string])[] = [
  [/干坤/g, '乾坤'],
  [/干隆/g, '乾隆'],
  [/干元/g, '乾元'],
  [/干爹/g, '乾爹'],
  [/干妈/g, '乾妈'],
];

export function normalizeForCompare(input: string, mode: NormalizeMode = 'preserve'): string {
  if (!input) return '';

  let s = input;

  // 1. 合文白名单：提前抽出，防止任何阶段被拆解（OpenCC 对合文一般不动，但加保险）
  const ligatureSlots: string[] = [];
  s = Array.from(s)
    .map((ch) => {
      if (LIGATURE_PRESERVE.has(ch)) {
        ligatureSlots.push(ch);
        return '\uE000' + (ligatureSlots.leng...(truncated)
```

MAS-2 is committed. Here's a summary of what was completed and verified:

**MAS-2 参考为准绳 — done:**

- **pg_trgm retrieval fix**: `rawSql` tagged template from `@neondatabase/serverless` correctly binds JS `string[]` as PostgreSQL `uuid[]` arrays — the previous `db.execute(sql`...ANY(${uuidArray})`)` produced `malformed array literal`
- **Punctuation stripping**: New `stripForTrigram()` in `normalize.ts` strips CJK punctuation before storing `text_normalized` (and before querying), lifting similarity from 0.52 → 1.0 for exact content matches
- **Four-state matchStatus**: MATCH (≥0.75) / PARTIAL_MATCH (≥0.40) / NOT_MATCH (<0.40 but hit) / NOT_FOUND_IN_REF (refs uploaded but no paragraph matched)
- **E2E confirmed**: 论语 quote → PARTIAL_MATCH sim=0.647, hit=true, snippet stored; non-论语 quotes → NOT_FOUND_IN_REF

**Roadmap**: m2 now at 50% (MAS-1 ✓ MAS-2 ✓). Next: MAS-3 (moderation rejection explicit UI) or MAS-2b (map.txt neutral tone lint).

```
const REJECTION_MARKERS = [
  '无法回答',
  '不便回应',
  '内容政策',
  '敏感话题',
  '抱歉',
  '很抱歉',
  '不能回答',
  '不宜回答',
  'content_filter',
  'content_policy',
  'safety',
  'redacted',
] as const;

interface RejectionProbe {
  readonly body?: unknown;
  readonly status?: number;
  readonly message?: string;
}

export function isModerationRejection(err: unknown): boolean {
  if (!err) return false;

  if (err instanceof Error) {
    return containsMarker(`${err.message}\n${err.stack ?? ''}`);
  }

  if (typeof err === 'object') {
    const probe = err as RejectionProbe;

    if (typeof probe.status === 'number' && probe.status >= 400) {
      if (containsMarker(safeSerialize(probe.body))) return true;
    }

    const content = extractChoiceContent(probe.body);
    if (content && containsMarker(content)) return true;

    if (containsMarker(safeSerialize(err))) return true;
  }

  return containsMarker(String(err));
}

function extractChoiceContent(body: unknown): string | null {
  if (!body || typeo...(truncated)
```
